573 // arrays of the CKD H2O, CO2, N2, O2 absorption models
575 
576 // additional array fields due to different numbering schemes of F77 and C/C++
577 const int addF77fields = 1;
578 
579 
580 /*
581  ---------------------------------------------------------------------
582 
583 c 29 August 2002
584 c
585 c This version, ckd_2.4.2, is composed of the updates to all continua
586 c including water vapor (ckd_2.2). This is to retain consistency between the
587 c continuum and the HITRAN line parameters.
588 c
589 
590  further information can be found under
591  http://www.rtweb.aer.com/continuum_frame.html
592 
593  Transformation from original F77 code to C/C++ by
594  T. Kuhn, iup Bremen, October 2003
595 
596  ---------------------------------------------------------------------
597  */
598 // H2O self continuum parameters at T=296 K for the CKD versions 0 to 2.4.2
599 // date of last update: 06/28/82
600 // units of (CM**3/MOL)*1.E-20
601 const Numeric SL296_ckd_0_v1 = -20.0;
602 const Numeric SL296_ckd_0_v2 = 20000.0;
603 const Numeric SL296_ckd_0_dv = 10.0;
604 const int SL296_ckd_0_npt = 2003;
605 const double SL296_ckd_0[SL296_ckd_0_npt+addF77fields] = {
606  0.0000e-00, 1.1109e-01, 1.0573e-01,
607  1.0162e-01, 1.0573e-01, 1.1109e-01, 1.2574e-01, 1.3499e-01, // f02740
608  1.4327e-01, 1.5065e-01, 1.5164e-01, 1.5022e-01, 1.3677e-01, // f02750
609  1.3115e-01, 1.2253e-01, 1.1271e-01, 1.0070e-01, 8.7495e-02, // f02760
610  8.0118e-02, 6.9940e-02, 6.2034e-02, 5.6051e-02, 4.7663e-02, // f02770
611  4.2450e-02, 3.6690e-02, 3.3441e-02, 3.0711e-02, 2.5205e-02, // f02780
612  2.2113e-02, 1.8880e-02, 1.6653e-02, 1.4626e-02, 1.2065e-02, // f02790
613  1.0709e-02, 9.1783e-03, 7.7274e-03, 6.7302e-03, 5.6164e-03, // f02800
614  4.9089e-03, 4.1497e-03, 3.5823e-03, 3.1124e-03, 2.6414e-03, // f02810
615  2.3167e-03, 2.0156e-03, 1.7829e-03, 1.5666e-03, 1.3928e-03, // f02820
616  1.2338e-03, 1.0932e-03, 9.7939e-04, 8.8241e-04, 7.9173e-04, // f02830
617  7.1296e-04, 6.4179e-04, 5.8031e-04, 5.2647e-04, 4.7762e-04, // f02850
618  4.3349e-04, 3.9355e-04, 3.5887e-04, 3.2723e-04, 2.9919e-04, // f02860
619  2.7363e-04, 2.5013e-04, 2.2876e-04, 2.0924e-04, 1.9193e-04, // f02870
620  1.7618e-04, 1.6188e-04, 1.4891e-04, 1.3717e-04, 1.2647e-04, // f02880
